tam abruvan yata idam ādithāḥ kim iha bhaviṣyatīti
so 'bravīc chandāṃsy atra prativapsyāmi chandobhir etā ākhyāyiṣyanta iti
yad abravīc chandāṃsy atra prativapsyāmi chandobhir etā ākhyāyiṣyanta iti tasmād etā gāyatrīḥ satīś chandobhir ākhyāyante
athopagītenaiva te 'yajanta
te sarva eva sāṅgāḥ satanavo 'mṛtāḥ samabhavan
sarvo haiva sāṅgaḥ satanur amṛtaḥ sambhavati ya evaṃ veda
etasmāt tad yad vidvāñchreyān bhavatīti ha smāha śāṭyāyaniḥ
athaitad āmahīyavaṃ prājāpatyaṃ savanamukhe kriyate
tad etat svayampraśastaṃ yat prājāpatyam
tasminn u praśasta eva saty eṣā bhūyasī praśaṃsā kriyate yad etad om ity ādatte
asau vā āditya etad akṣaram
tad etat trayasya vedasyāpīḍitam akṣaram
sa yad om ity ādatte 'mum evaitad ādityaṃ mukha ādhatte
sa yathā madhunā lājān prayuyād evam evaitenākṣareṇa sāman rasaṃ dadhāti
tad āpyāyayati
tenāsyāpīnena rasavatā stutaṃ bhavati
pratihriyamāṇaṃ sāmāvasīdatīty āhuḥ kuravaḥ
sa yad ūrdhvaṃ pratihārād udgṛhṇāti tad utthāpayatīti
sāmann u haivaitat sāmābhigīyate
taddha vai sugītaṃ yat sāman sāmābhigāyāt
sāmann evedaṃ sāmābhigāyāmīty eva tad vidyāc chreṣṭhatām anena svānāṃ gamiṣyāmīti
punānaḥ soma dhārayeti prastauti
apo vasāno arṣasīty aṣṭāv akṣarāṇi
ā ratnadhā yonim ṛtasya satety aṣṭau
tāni ṣoḍaśa
sya sīdasīti catvāri
tato yāni ṣoḍaśa sa eva ṣoḍaśakalaḥ paśuḥ
atha yāni catvāri ta etasya paśoḥ stanāḥ
sa yathā paśuṃ staninaṃ prattaṃ duhītaivam evaitena gītenaitad duhe yaṃ kāmaṃ kāmayate
tat paśavyam iti ha smāha sucittaś śailanaḥ
sa paśumān bhavati ya evaṃ vidvān rauravaṃ gāyatīti
prastūyamānaṃ sāma prajākāmo 'bhyudgāyet
vihṛte prastāve kṣatrakāmaḥ
pratihriyamāṇam eva paśukāmo 'bhyudgāyet
nidhanam eva svaram upayan brahmavarcasaṃ dhyāyet
brahmavarcasaṃ hi svaraḥ
te catvāraḥ sāman kāmā iti ha smāha jānaśruteyaḥ
atha ha smāha vaitahavyas traya eva sāman kāmāḥ
yad eva vācā karoti sā prajā
manaso hi vāk prajāyate
sa yad vācā karomi prajā ma eṣā prajāvān etena bhaviṣyāmīty eva tad vidyāt
atha yad ṛcaṃ gāyati te paśavaḥ
paśavo hy ṛk
sa yad ṛcaṃ gāyāmi paśavo ma ete paśumān etena bhaviṣyāmīty eva tad vidyāt
atha yan nidhanaṃ svaram upaiti tad brahmavarcasam
brahmavarcasaṃ hi svaraḥ
sa yan nidhanaṃ svaram upaimi brahmavarcasaṃ ma etad brahmavarcasy etena bhaviṣyāmīty eva tad vidyāt
atraivaite sarve kāmā upāpyanta evaṃ viduṣa iti
tad etat satyam akṣaraṃ yad om iti
vajrā ha khalu vā ete yad yaudhājayasya sāmno nidhanāni
te devā etena satyenābhigīyom om ity etair yaudhājayasya nidhanair asurān pāpmānaṃ bhrātṛvyān aghnan
evam evaivaṃ vidvān etena satyenābhigīyom om ity etair yaudhājayasya nidhanair dviṣantaṃ pāpmānaṃ bhrātṛvyaṃ hanti
tat triṇidhanaṃ bhavati
trayo vā ime lokāḥ
vajrā ete yan nidhanāni
ebhyo lokebhya etair vajraiḥ sarvaṃ pāpmānam apahate
atho hāsyaita eva vajrā eṣu lokeṣu sarvaṃ pāpmānam apahatyom ity eva svargaṃ lokam ārohati
athaitad auśanaṃ traiṣṭubham
tad yatra devāsurāḥ saṃyattā āsaṃs tad eṣām abravīt trir ahaṃ ṣṭub asmīti
yad abravīt trir ahaṃ ṣṭub asmīti tasmāt triṣṭup
te devā etayā triḥ stutvāsurān pāpmānaṃ bhrātṛvyān aghnan
evam evaivaṃ vidvān etayā triḥ stutvā dviṣantaṃ pāpmānaṃ bhrātṛvyaṃ hanti
tasya triḥ prarohati
traiṣṭubho vā asāv ādityaś śuklaṃ kṛṣṇaṃ puruṣaḥ
traiṣṭubham idaṃ cakṣuś śuklaṃ kṛṣṇaṃ puruṣaḥ
tacchreṣṭhayā devatayā sampādyodgāyati
sa śreṣṭhatāṃ svānām aśnute ya evaṃ vidvān auśanaṃ gāyatīti
atha nirbādhāpastambhau
sāmno hiṃkriyamāṇa etāṃ diśaṃ yaṃ dviṣyāt taṃ manasā nirbādheta
tata eva sa parābhavati
pratihriyamāṇa etām u eva diśaṃ yaṃ dviṣyāt taṃ manasāpastabhnuyāt
tata u eva sa parābhavati
atho trayaḥ sāmnaḥ svargās trayo nārakāḥ
prastute purādeḥ sa nārakaḥ
tad dviṣantaṃ bhrātṛvyaṃ pātayitvā ādiḥ svargo lokas tasminn ātmānaṃ dadhyāt
pratihṛte puropadravāt sa nārakaḥ
tad dviṣantaṃ bhrātṛvyaṃ pātayitvā upadravaḥ svargo lokas tasminn ātmānaṃ dadhyāt
upadrute purā nidhanāt sa nārakaḥ
tad dviṣantaṃ bhrātṛvyaṃ pātayitvā nidhanaṃ svargo lokas tasminn ātmānaṃ dadhyāt
tad u hovāca śāṭyāyanir apahatapāpmaitat sāmno yad ūrdhvaṃ prastāvāt
svarga eṣa lokaḥ
kas tasmin dviṣantaṃ bhrātṛvyam ābhajet
prastuta eva purādeḥ sa evaiko nārakaḥ
tad dviṣantaṃ bhrātṛvyaṃ pātayitvā sarvasminn eva sāmann ātmānaṃ dadhyāt
atho yajamānam
so 'pahatya pāpmānaṃ svargaṃ lokam eti
etat tad yat kṛtvā śreyān manyata iti
yo vā ṛksāmābhyām āyatanavadbhyām ārtvijyaṃ karoty āyatanavān bhavati
prastāva evarcaḥ sāmann āyatanam
yad ūrdhvaṃ prastāvāc channaṃ gāyati tat sāmna ṛcy āyatanam
pratihāra evarcaḥ sāmann āyatanam
yad ūrdhvaṃ pratihārāc channaṃ gāyati tat sāmna ṛcy āyatanam
nidhanam evarcaḥ sāmann āyatanam
yan nidhanam atisvarati tat sāmna ṛcy āyatanam
sa ya evam etābhyām ṛksāmābhyām āyatanavadbhyām ārtvijyaṃ karoty āyatanavān eva bhavati
tad vā etad dvayam evark caiva sāma ca
tayor yat satyaṃ prajāsu bhavati jayati taṃ lokaṃ yaḥ satyena jeyaḥ
vāg vā ṛcaḥ satyam
manaḥ sāmnaḥ
ete ha vā ṛksāmayoḥ satye
satyaṃ prajāsu bhavati jayati taṃ lokaṃ yaḥ satyena jeyaḥ
ṛcaḥ satyena sāma gāyāt
sāmnaḥ satyenarcam
ṛksāmne u ha vai svargasya lokasyeśāte
taṃ ha vā ete svargaṃ lokaṃ gamayataḥ
sa svargasya lokasyeśe ya ene evaṃ gāyati
tasmād evam eva geye
rathantareṇa stoṣyamāṇaḥ pṛthivīm abhimṛśati namo mātre pṛthivyai rathantara mā mā hiṃsīr iti
atha mahimnaḥ saṃbharati yas te agnau mahimā yas te apsu rathe yas te mahimā stanayitnau ya u te vāte yas te mahimā tena saṃbhava rathantara draviṇasvan na edhīti
atha vāmadevyaṃ purastāc chāntim abhivyāharati prajāpatir asi vāmadevya brahmaṇaś śaraṇa tan mā pāhīti
athaitā amṛtavyāhṛtīr abhivyāharati bhūr bhuvaḥ svaḥ ka idam udgāsyati sa idam udgāsyatīti
prajāpatir vai kaḥ
tam evādāv ārtvijyāya vṛṇīte
sa ya eva tad udgāyati vācaivāsya kṛtaṃ bhavati
anṛṇa ātmanā bhavati
athābhyaniti
prāṇo vai śāntiḥ
agnir vai bṛhadrathantare
te prāṇena śamayati
atha ye 'śānte bṛhadrathantare gāyanti te haite yuvānaś śrotriyāḥ pramīyante svayam upariṣṭād vāmadevyam
sa yathā gharmaṃ taptaṃ śaphābhyāṃ parigṛhya hared evam evaitad bṛhadrathantare vāmadevyābhyāṃ parigṛhya harati
te enaṃ nodoṣataḥ
sa sarvam āyur eti ya evaṃ vidvān bṛhadrathantare gāyati
iyaṃ vai rathantaram
tasyā asau vatso yo 'sau tapati
sa yad bhā bhā iti stobdhy etam eva tad ādityaṃ mukha ādhāya gāyati
sa yathā dhenuṃ vatsenopasṛjya prattāṃ duhītaivam evaitena gītena rathantaraṃ duhe yaṃ kāmaṃ kāmayate
śrīr vai rathantaram
tasyā ime stobhā yad asyāṃ pṛthivyām adhi
saiṣā śrīr nānyatrākṣarebhya āptavyā
sa yad akṣareṣu stobdhy etām eva tacchriyam āptvaitasyāṃ pratitiṣṭhati
sā haiṣaikasthā śrīr yad akṣareṣu
tasmād akṣareṣu stobdhavyam
tad etad amūlaṃ rathantaraṃ yad anyatrākṣarebhyaḥ
etasmāddhīdam āyatanāt pracyavante ye 'nyatrākṣarebhyaḥ stobhanti
atha yo 'kṣareṣu stobdhi sva eva tad āyatane pratitiṣṭhati
tasmād akṣareṣv eva stobdhavyam
devatāgāyinaḥ kurupañcālā āyatanād acyavanteti ha smāha śāṭyāyaniḥ
mano vai pūrvam atha vāk
mano vai bṛhad vāg rathantaram
tad yatra bṛhadrathantare ājim aitāṃ tad bṛhad udajayat
rathantaraṃ hīyamānam amanyata
tad yat kṣipraṃ rathantaraṃ gāyati manaś caiva tad vācaṃ ca same karoti
tad idaṃ rathantaram īkṣate yo mām anena samam akṛddhantāyaṃ kṣipre pāpmānaṃ vijahātv iti
sa ha kṣipre pāpmānaṃ vijahāti ya evaṃ vidvān kṣipraṃ rathantaraṃ gāyati
tat pūrṇamukhenāpradhūnvan kṣipraṃ gāyet
śrīr eṣā yad rathantaram
śriyam etad ātman dhatte
atho agnir eṣa yad rathantaram
tasmāt kṣipraṃ mumukṣitavyam
yatra vā agnir upatiṣṭhamāno dahati dūra iva vai tatrauṣadhayaḥ prajāyante
yatropadhūnvann eti kṣipraṃ tatrauṣadhayaḥ prajāyante
kṣipraṃ prajayā paśubhiḥ prajāyā iti pratihāre pratihāra udgāteḍeti brūyāt
paśavo vā iḍā
āyatanaṃ rathantaram
āyatana eva tad etān paśūn pratiṣṭhāpayati
taddhaitad eka ekarūpam eva bhā bhā iti stobhanti
asau vā ādityo bhā iti
tad u hovāca śāṭyāyanir amithunam etad aprajananaṃ yad ekarūpam
bhago vā asau
bhid iyam
pumān vā asau
strīyam
yadā vā asau varṣaty atheyaṃ prajāyate
yado vai pumān yoṣāyāṃ retaḥ siñcaty atha sā prajāyate
tasmād abhubhābhibhabhebhabha ity eva mithunaṃ prajananaṃ stobdhavyam
yāvat stobhet tāvat pṛthivyāṃ hastau syātāṃ devarathasyānapavyāthāya
ṣoḍaśākṣarāṇi stobhati
ṣoḍaśakalo vai puruṣaḥ
kalāśa eva tad yajamānam etasyāṃ devayonyāṃ siñcati
sa etasyai devayonyai jāyate devān adhi
caturdaśa caturdaśottarayoḥ
tato yāni daśa sā virāṭ
annaṃ virāṭ
atha yāni catvāri ta eva catuṣpadāḥ paśavaḥ
tac catuṣpadaḥ paśūn avarunddhe
ṣoḍaśākṣarāṇi stobhati
tato yāni pañcadaśa sa vajraḥ pañcadaśaḥ
atha yat ṣoḍaśam akṣaraṃ sa indraḥ
indro vajrasyodyantā ṣoḍaśaḥ
tam indraṃ yajamānam akṛt
tad udgātā yajamānasya pañcadaśena vajreṇa dviṣantaṃ pāpmānaṃ bhrātṛvyaṃ stṛṇāti
caturdaśa caturdaśottarayoḥ
sa ha sa vajra ūnonārambhaṇaḥ
tad udgātā yajamānasya bhrātṛvyāyatane bhrātṛvyaṃ vitakṣṇoti bhrātṛvyāyatane bhrātṛvyaṃ vināśaṃ nayati
na hāsya kaścana bhrātṛvyo bhavati ya evaṃ veda
ṣoḍaśākṣarāṇi stobhati
caturdaśa caturdaśottarayoḥ
tāni catuścatvāriṃśad akṣarāṇi sampadyante
catuścatvāriṃśadakṣarā triṣṭup
traiṣṭubha indraḥ
sa ha sa indraś chandasāṃ madhyataḥ prāvasito bahūni chandāṃsi purastād bahūny upariṣṭāt
chandāṃsi vai sarve stomāḥ sarve paśavaḥ sarve devāḥ sarve lokāḥ sarve kāmāḥ
tat sarvān stomān sarvān paśūn sarvān devān sarvān lokān sarvān kāmān āpnoti
agnir eṣa yad rathantaram
agnir vai mṛtyuḥ
sa yo 'nyatrākṣarebhyaḥ stobdhi sa evodgātā yajamānaṃ mṛtyor āsye 'pyasyati
atha yo 'kṣareṣu stobdhy annam u vai stobhas stobhena stobhenaiva mṛtyor āsyam apidhāyaitaṃ mṛtyum atitarati
atho samudra eṣa yad rathantaram
atha yo 'nyatrākṣarebhyaḥ stobdhi sa evaitaṃ samudraṃ praviśati
atha yo 'kṣareṣu stobdhi yathā nāvā vā plavena vā dvīpād dvīpaṃ saṃkrāmed evam evaitaṃ samudram atitarati
svardṛśam iti nirāha
yadā vai svar gacchaty athāmṛto bhavati
taṃ sarvebhyo devebhyaḥ sarvebhyo bhūtebhyaḥ prāha svar ayaṃ brāhmaṇo 'gann amṛto 'bhūd iti
sa taṃ sarve devāḥ sarvāṇi bhūtāny anubudhyante
athaitad vāmadevyam
ā pratihārād anavānaṃ geyam
prāṇo hi vāmadevyam
prāṇān ned avacchidyāmahā iti
no hānyasyānuvartma geyam
īśvaro hopajīvī bhavitor yo 'nyasyānuvartma gāyati
svadhūr eva geyam
taddha smāha brahmadattaś caikitāneyo rūkṣitam ivaitad yad vāmadevyaṃ nirdhūtam iva
sāmāni hy asmāt sṛṣṭāni
yathā jaratkośo vā syād aśvataro vā vicchidvahāḥ
pṛṣṭhaṃ pṛṣṭhaṃ hi prativahatīti
tasmin pṛṣṭharūpaṃ vā gāyed etā vā vyāhṛtīr vyāhṛtyodgāyed gauś cāśvaś cājā cāviś ca vrīhiś ca yavaś ceti
gaur eva rathantaram
aśvo bṛhat
ajā vairūpam
avir vairājam
vrīhayaś śakvaryaḥ
yavā revatayaḥ
tad ye 'smād rasāt sṛṣṭā bhavanti tān asmin dadhāti
tad āpyāyayati
tenāsyāpīnena rasavatā stutaṃ bhavati
sa yadi vṛṣṭikāmaḥ syād āpo vāyur āpo vāyur iti purastād vyāhṛtya vāmadevyena stuvīta
tatho haivāsmai varṣati
atho paśavo vai vāmadevyam
sa paśumān bhavati ya evaṃ vidvān vāmadevyena stute
taddha vai sugītaṃ brahmasāmno yad enad brahmalokaiḥ sampādyodgāyati
sapta kṛtvo brahmasāmnaḥ prarohati
saptama u loke brahma
vāsor māndāno vā iti catuḥ prārukṣat
āndhāsā bhī vātsān no vā iti triḥ
tat sapta sampadyante
upodako nāma loko yasminn ayam agniḥ
ṛtadhāmā yasmin vāyuḥ
aparājito yasminn ādityaḥ
adhidyur yasmin varuṇaḥ
pradyur yasmin mṛtyuḥ
rocano yasminn aśanāyā
viṣṭapa eva saptamo brahmaloko yasminn etad brahma
tat saptamena praroheṇa viṣṭape brahmaloka ātmānaṃ dadhyāt
atho yajamānam
atho hainad gamayati
yad enat spṛśatīva taddhainat priyeṇa dhāmnā samardhayati
yaddha sma sucittaś śailana udgṛhṇāti svāsarāyiṣū dhenovā ity abhi brahmalokam ārohayati priyeṇa dhāmnā samardhayati
tad u hainat samṛddhaṃ priyeṇo eva dhāmnā samardhayati
tad v imaṃ lokam āgamayati
teno sarvam āyur eti
athaitat kāleyam
vistṛṇann iva vyavasāyayann ivāsaṃrundhann iva gāyet
yathā yavācitaṃ vā svācitaṃ yāyān māṣācitaṃ veti ha sma purā kurūṇāṃ brāhmaṇā mīmāṃsanta evam etad yat kāleyam
tad vikarṣateva geyam iti
taddhaitad eke rathantarasāmna ūrdhvām iḍām upayanti nakāriṇām oyiḍā iti
tad u hovāca śāṭyāyanir uddhatevaiṣeḍā pracyuteva
nitatām eveḍām antata upayan bṛhatsāmno dvitīyasyai stotriyāyai dhoro ity udgṛhṇīyāt
tad eva bṛhato rūpān na yanti
atha haike rathantarasāmnaś caiva bṛhatsāmnaś cordhvām eveḍām upayanty anavadhmātaiṣeḍā svargyeti
tad u hovāca śāṭyāyanir agnir vai rathantaram
vāyur vāmadevyam
indro naudhasam
viśve devāḥ kāleyam
athaiṣa svarga eva loko viśva eva devāḥ
svarga eva tal loke viśveṣu deveṣu pratitiṣṭhanti
sa ya enāṃs tathā cakruṣo 'nuvyāhared iti veti vā bhaviṣyantīti tathā haiva syuḥ
tasmād eṣā nitataiveḍāntata upetyā sarvāyuṣṭāyā asya lokasyānudghātāyeti
athaitat saṃhitaṃ brahma savanamukhe kriyate
tad etat svayampraśastaṃ yad brahma
tasminn u praśasta eva saty eṣā bhūyasī praśaṃsā kriyate yad etad om ity ādatte
asāv āditya etad akṣaram
tad etat trayasya vedasyāpīḍitam akṣaram
sa yad om ity ādatte 'mum evaitad ādityaṃ mukha ādhatte
sa yathā madhunā lājān prayuyād evam evaitenākṣareṇa sāman rasaṃ dadhāti
tad āpyāyayati
tenāsyāpīnena rasavatā stutaṃ bhavati
pratihriyamāṇaṃ sāmāvasīdatīty āhuḥ kuravaḥ
sa yad ūrdhvaṃ pratihārād udgṛhṇāti tad utthāpayatīti
sāmann u haivaitat sāmābhigīyate
taddha vai sugītam
yat sāman sāmābhigāyāt sāmann evedaṃ sāmābhigāyāmīty eva tad vidyāc chreṣṭhatām anena svānāṃ gamiṣyāmīti
athaite uṣṇikkakubhāv ā pratihārād anavānaṃ geye
saṃśīrṇam ivaitac chandaḥ
puruṣacchandasaṃ hy uṣṇikkakubhau
taddha śamastomī bālākiḥ sāyakaṃ jānaśruteyam antevāsinam udgāpayan svayajñe 'nuvyājahāra
tathā nvā ayaṃ jānaśruteyaḥ sāmāgāsīd yathāsyedānīṃ rudhiram utpatiṣyatīti
atha hājinavāsino yudhyamānāḥ sadaḥ prapeduḥ
tasya ha daṇḍaḥ patitvā rudhiram utpātayāṃcakāra
sa hovācātha kathaṃ gāyed iti
tasmai haitad uvācāsṛg ity eva na nirdyotayet
ho ity eva gāyet
no ha sarvaṃ tṛtīyasavanaṃ channaṃ gāyet
yo hainaṃ chādayantaṃ brūyād adhakṣan vā ayam udgātātmānaṃ ca yajamānaṃ ceti tathā haiva syāt
dṛṃhyām eva nirdyotayet
dṛṃhīmān iti vai praśaṃsanti
athaitac chyāvāśvam
aiho vā ehi yā ity evaite gāyanti
vāg eṣā
vāg anuṣṭup
vācy etad vācā pratitiṣṭhāmeti
taddha tathā gāyantaṃ brahmadattaṃ caikitāneyaṃ gaḍūnā ārkṣākāyaṇo 'nuvyājahāra
tathā nvā ayaṃ dālbhyaś śyāvāśvam agāsīd yathainaṃ svaḥ pāpmābhyārokṣyatīti
tad u hetaro 'nubudhyovāca tatho vāva sa vāmadevyam agāyad yathā rūkṣa evāpaśuś cariṣyatīti
atha ha brahmadattaṃ caikitāneyaṃ brahmadattaḥ prāsenajitaḥ
kausalyo rājā puro dadhe
tasya ha putraḥ prācyavad babhāṣe
sa hovāca pramayo vā ayam
yuktam eva punar yāsyāmīti
sa ha prayayau
atha hāsya jaimavaṃ sajātaṃ vailūnaya āninyire
teṣāṃ ha samitim ājagāma
sa ha sa tṛṇebhyo 'nūttasthau
utpatati ha sma purā
taṃ ha bahu pradāya babādhe
tau samājagmatuḥ
sa hovācetthaṃ ced idam abhūt
ehīdaṃ saṃprabravāvahā iti
sa hovāca gaḍūnāś śyāvāśvaṃ vā ārcanānasaṃ samiddhāraṃ paretaṃ pratisattriṇo hitvā svargaṃ lokam āyan
taṃ hainaṃ śyāvāśvenaivaiho vā ehy ā ity udāhvayan
hīna ivaiṣa yaḥ sajātaḥ
sa yad ai ho vā ehy ā iti gāyati svenaivainat tat pāpmanābhyārohayata iti
tasmai haitad uvāco ho i yā ity eva gāyet
o ho vai nāmendraḥ
ya evāsau tapaty eṣa evendraḥ
sa u eva yas tasya sarve devā anuvartmānaḥ
sarve hāsya svā anuvartmāno bhavanti ya evaṃ vidvāñchyāvāśvaṃ gāyatīti
athaitad āndhīgavaṃ madhyenidhanaṃ pratiṣṭhāyai
tad yad evātra yajñasya duṣṣṭutaṃ duśśastaṃ vidhuraṃ tad evaitenānuvaste
athaitasya kāvasya pañca kṛtvaḥ prarohati
pañcapadā vai paṅktiḥ
pāṅktāḥ paśavaḥ
paśavo jagatī
tān etān paśuṣu paśūn vitanoti
tat paśavyam iti ha smāha sucittaś śailanaḥ
sa paśumān bhavati nāsya tantiḥ kulāc chidyate ya evaṃ vidvān kāvaṃ gāyatīti
tantir iti ha smaitad gītam ācaṣṭe
atho svargasya lokasya vyāptir iti
iyaṃ vai gāyatrī
antarikṣaṃ triṣṭup
asau jagatī
tat tṛtīyena praroheṇa svargaṃ lokam ārohati
tat paśavyaṃ svargyam iti ha smāha
etāv ubhau kāmāv upāpnoti
yo vai yajñasyodhar veda prattaṃ yajñaṃ duhe
yajñāyajñīyaṃ vāva yajñasyodhaḥ
tasyaite stanā gāyatraṃ ca rathantaraṃ ca bṛhac ca vāmadevyaṃ ca
tad gāyatram iva prastuyāt
rathantarasyeva stobhān stobhet
bṛhata iva rohān rohet
hiṃkāro vāmadevyam
svayam eva yajñāyajñīyam
etad vai yajñaṃ yajamāno duhe
sa heṣṭvaiva śreyān bhavati
tasya daśa kṛtvaḥ prarohati
ṣaṭ kṛtvaḥ pūrvayoḥ
catur uttamāyai
te daśa prarohāḥ sampadyante
daśākṣarā virāṭ
annaṃ virāṭ
ya evāsau tapaty eṣa eva virāṭ
etasminn eva tat svarge loke 'ntataḥ pratitiṣṭhanti
athokthāni channamiśrāṇīva gāyet
ahno hy ukthāni
atha rātrim āvir eva gāyet
channeva hi rātriḥ
tad āhur udgātar ahan rātrim agāsī3 rātryām ahā3r iti
ubhayam iti brūyād ahann eva rātrim agāsiṣaṃ rātryām ahar iti
āvir vā ahaḥ
tasmin yac channaṃ gāyati mithunam eva tat prajananaṃ dadhāti
channā vai rātriḥ
tāṃ yad āvir gāyati yathā tamasi jyotir dadhyāt tādṛk tat
tasmād rātryā eva rūpeṇāhar gāyed ahno rūpeṇa rātrim
tad eva sūdgītam
atho ahorātre eva tad anyonyasmin pratiṣṭhāpayan gāyati
tad yad ahar āviḥ sat tac channaṃ gāyati tasmād asāv āditya idaṃ sarvaṃ na pradahati
atha yad rātriṃ channāṃ satīṃ tām āvir gāyati tasmād u hedaṃ naktaṃ kiṃ ca nirjñāyate
yaddha tāṃ channām eva gāyed andham eva tamaḥ syāt
atha rājāno 'gniṣṭomasāmāni
rājaputrā dvādaśāhīyāni
viśaś chandasyāni
tasmād etāni trayāṇi sāmāni saṃvatsare kāryāṇi
yad vai kṣatraṃ viḍvad rājaputravad bhavati tat samṛddham
sa yathā kṣatraṃ viḍvad rājaputravat syāt tādṛk tat
tad yad etāni sāmāni saṃvatsare kriyante 'thāto 'gniṣṭomasāmnām eva gānam
yathā rājñaḥ pariṣkāraś śāmūlājinaṃ maṇihiraṇyaṃ hastī niṣko 'śvatarīratho 'śvaratho rukmaḥ kaṃsas ta evam eṣa eteṣāṃ sāmnāṃ pariṣkāraḥ
tasmād agniṣṭomasāmāny eva gānīkṛtya gāyed yathāgītam itarāṇi yathāgītam itarāṇi
yadi somau saṃsutau syātāṃ mahārātre prātaranuvākam upākuryāt
pūrvo vācaṃ pūrvo devatāḥ pūrvaś chandāṃsi vṛṅkte
chandāṃsi vai sarvā devatāḥ
sarvā evaiṣāṃ devatā vṛñjate
pūrvo vasatīvarīr jigrahayiṣet
etā vai sarvā devatā yad vasatīvaryaḥ
sarvā evaiṣāṃ devatā vṛñjate
suṣamiddhe hotavyam
agnir vai sarvā devatāḥ
sarvā u eva tad devatāḥ paśyanto yajante chandobhyo 'bhibhūtyai
āgnīdhre hotavyam
saṃveśāyopaveśāya gāyatryai chandase 'bhibhūtyai svāheti prātassavane juhuyāt
saṃveśāyopaveśāya triṣṭubhe chandase 'bhibhūtyai svāheti mādhyaṃdine savane juhuyāt
saṃveśāyopaveśāya jagatyai chandase 'bhibhūtyai svāheti tṛtīyasavane juhuyāt
chandobhir vai devā asurān abhyabhavan
sapatnāyantīvaite ye saṃsunvanti
chandobhir evainān abhibhavanti
prajāpater ṛgbhir hotavyam
prajāpatir vai sarvā devatāḥ
sarvā evaiṣāṃ devatā vṛñjate
yadi kāmayerann adhvaryur eṣāṃ mriyetety adhvaryuṃ prātassavane brūyuḥ prajāpater ṛgbhir juhudhīti
yadi kāmayeran hotaiṣāṃ mriyeteti hotāraṃ mādhyaṃdine savane brūyuḥ prajāpater ṛgbhir juhudhīti
yadi kāmayerann udgātaiṣāṃ mriyetety udgātāraṃ tṛtīyasavane brūyuḥ prajāpater ṛgbhir juhudhīti
evamāyatanā vā ṛtvijaḥ
adhvaryuḥ prathamo yujyate
tasya prātassavanam āyatanam
atha hotā
tasya mādhyaṃdinaṃ savanam āyatanam
athodgātā
tasya tṛtīyasavanam āyatanam
yathāyatanam evainān spṛṇvate
yadi kāmayeran yajamāna eṣāṃ mriyeteti yajamānaṃ brūyuḥ prajāpater ṛgbhir juhudhīti
yadi kāmayeran sarva eva mriyerann iti sarva eva sarveṣu savaneṣu juhuyuḥ
ubhe bṛhadrathantare bhavataḥ
indrasya vā etau harī yad ubhe bṛhadrathantare
yajño devarathaḥ
indrasyaiva haribhyāṃ yajñena devarathenājim ujjayati
idaṃ vai rathantaram
ado bṛhat
asmād amuṣmād adyaśvāt mithunād evainān antaryanti
pra vo vājā abhidyava ity āgneyam ājyaṃ bhavati
pravat tyad devatānāṃ rūpam abhibhūtyai rūpam
abhy evainān bhavanti
ābhīkam abhinidhanam abhīvartam ābhīśavam ity etāni sāmāni bhavanty abhibhūtyai rūpam
abhy evainān bhavanti
vihavīyaṃ sajanīyam agastyasya kayāśubhīyam ity etāni śastrāṇi bhavanti
tato yad vihavīyam indram eva tena devatānām āhvayante
sam evainaṃ sajanīyena vṛñjate
agastyaṃ vai rakṣāṃsi anvasacanta
so 'kāmayatāpa rakṣāṃsi hanīyeti
sa etat kayāśubhīyaṃ śastram apaśyat
tena rakṣāṃsy apāghnata
rakṣāṃsīva vā etān sacante ye saṃsunvanti
tad yat kayāśubhīyaṃ śastraṃ bhavati rakṣasām evāpahatyai
yadītare 'gniṣṭomaṃ kurvīrann athātmanokthyaṃ kurvīran
yadītara ukthyaṃ kurvīrann athātmanā ṣoḍaśinaṃ gṛhṇīran
yadītare ṣoḍaśinaṃ gṛhṇīrann athātmanātirātraṃ kurvīran
yadītare 'tirātraṃ kurvīrann athātmanā dvirātraṃ kurvīran
yadītare dvirātraṃ kurvīrann athātmanā trirātraṃ kurvīran
bhūyāṃsi stotrāṇi bhūyāṃsi śastrāṇi bhūyasīr devatā upayanty abhibhūtyai rūpam
abhy evainān bhavanti
yathā ha vā idaṃ senayoḥ saṃtiṣṭhamānayor anu yodhā bhūyāṃsa āyanti tādṛk tat
tad u vā āhur imam evāgre manasā yajñakratum ākuveta
tam evojjigīṣet
yo vai saha palāyitayoḥ pūrvaḥ kāṣṭhāṃ gacchati sa vāva tayor jayati
pūrva eva saṃsthāṃ prepsed iti
yadi dīkṣitānāṃ pramīyeta taṃ dagdhvāsthāny upanahyāpabhajya somaṃ yo 'sya nediṣṭhatamaḥ syāt tena saha dīkṣayitvā yājayeyuḥ
samānāya vā ete yajñāya samānāya sukṛtāya samārabhya dīkṣante
tenaivainaṃ niravadayante
etad anyat kuryuḥ
abhiṣutya somam anyad agṛhītvā grahān yā dakṣiṇāḥ sraktīs tad asthāni nidhāya mārjālīye stuvīran
arbudasyargbhiḥ stuvate
arbudo vai sarpaḥ
etābhir mṛtāṃ tvacam apāhata
mriyanta iva vā ete ye mṛtāya kurvantīti
mṛtām evaitābhis tvacam apaghnate
tisṛṣu stuvanti
tṛtīyo vā itaḥ pitṛlokaḥ
pitṛlokam evainaṃ gamayanti
parācīṣu stuvanti
parāñcam evainaṃ tad amuṃ lokaṃ gamayanti
yāmaṃ sāma bhavati
yamalokam evainaṃ gamayanti
aprastutam apratihṛtaṃ sāma bhavati
prastāvapratihārābhyāṃ vai yajamāno dhṛtaḥ
tad yad aprastutam apratihṛtaṃ sāma bhavaty amuṣminn evainaṃ tal loke pratiṣṭhāpayanti
stutam anuśaṃsanty etā ṛco 'nubruvanto dakṣiṇān ūrūn upāghnānāḥ
trir apasalī mārjālīyaṃ paryāyanti
amuṣminn evainaṃ tal loke nidhuvate
abhy enam amuṣmin loke vāyuḥ pavate
tad āhur yanti vā ete patho ye mṛtāya kurvantīti
aindravāyavāgrān grahān gṛhṇanti
punaḥ panthānaṃ paryavayanti
asaṃmitaṃ sarvaṃ stotraṃ bhavati
asaṃmito hy asau lokaḥ
amum evaitena lokam upasīdanti
tad āhus trivṛta eva pavamānāḥ syuḥ
saptadaśāny uttarāṇi stotrāṇi
prāṇā vai trivṛtaḥ
prāṇair vā ete vyṛdhyante ye mṛtāya kurvantīti
tad yat trivṛtaḥ pavamānā bhavanti prāṇair eva tat samṛdhyante
saptadaśāny uttarāṇi stotrāṇi
prajāpatir vai saptadaśaḥ
prajāpatiḥ svargasya lokasyābhinetā
sa yaḥ svargasya lokasyābhinetā sa mā svargaṃ lokam abhinayād iti
saptadaśā u evānyat pavamānāḥ syuḥ
trivṛnty uttarāṇi stotrāṇi
abhihvātāraṃ vāva mukha ṛcchanti
tad yathā prathamenaivaṃ hy arvāṅ ity abhihvayet tādṛk tat
trivṛnty uttarāṇi
prāṇā vai trivṛtaḥ
prāṇān eva tad abhyutkrāmanto yanti
tad āhur vīva vā ete prāṇāpānābhyām ṛdhyante ye mṛtāya kurvantīti
maitrāvaruṇāgrān grahān gṛhṇanti
prāṇāpānau vai mitrāvaruṇau
prāṇāpānābhyām eva tat samṛdhyante
tad āhur na purā saṃvatsarād asthāni yājyāni
yat purā saṃvatsarād asthāni yājayeyur vācaṃ krūrām aruṣkṛtām ṛccheyuḥ
upariṣṭād eva saṃvatsarasyāsthāni yājyāni
vācaṃ krūrām aruṣkṛtāṃ ned ṛcchāmeti
atho khalv āhur yatraivetare 'vabhṛtham abhyaveyus tad asthāny avahareyuḥ
samā hi vā eteṣāṃ yuktiś ca vimuktiś ca
yaivāmīṣāṃ vimuktis tām evānuvimucyata iti
yadi sāmi sattrād uttiṣṭheyur viśvajitātirātreṇa sarvapṛṣṭhena sarvavedasena yajeran
ṛtavo vai pṛṣṭhāni
saṃvatsara ṛtavaḥ
tenaivaiṣāṃ saṃvatsara āpto bhavati
atha yā dakṣiṇā dadati tābhir atiprayuñjate
atho khalv āhur ya evāyaṃ vaiśvānaraḥ prāyaṇīyo 'tirātras tenaiva yajerann iti
ahorātre vai parivartamāne saṃvatsaram āpnutaḥ
tenaivaiṣāṃ saṃvatsara āpto bhavati
atha yā dakṣiṇā dadati tābhir atiprayuñjate
yady ekasmin paryāye 'stute 'bhivyucchet pañcadaśabhir hotre stuyuḥ pañcabhiḥ pañcabhir itarebhyaḥ
yadi dvayoḥ paryāyayor astutayor abhivyuccheddhotre ca maitrāvaruṇāya ca pūrve stuyur brahmaṇe cācchāvākāya cottare
yadi sarveṣu paryāyeṣv astuteṣv abhivyucchet ṣaḍbhir hotre stuyus tisṛbhis tisṛbhir itarebhyaḥ
sarvebhya etad anyat kuryuḥ
ekādaśān yad ekarcān upetyaindraṃ dvādaśaṃ sarvaṃ tṛcam
evaṃ ha cakre mauñjaḥ sāhaśravasaḥ
tam u ha kapivano bhauvāyana uvācāgavāyanībhir iva bata mahā sāhaśravaso 'gāt
unmadiṣṇur asya prajā bhaviṣyati
brahmavarcasinī tv eva bhaviṣyatīti
yan mām āmantrayiṣyateti hovāca dvādaśaivaitān ekarcān upetyaindraṃ dvādaśam agne vivasvad uṣasa ity etasmiṃs tṛce rāthantaraṃ saṃdhim astoṣyat
agna iti tenāgneyād rūpān naiṣyat
uṣasa ity uṣasyāt
sajūr aśvibhyām ity āśvināt
nāsyonmadiṣṇuḥ prajābhaviṣyat
brahmavarcasinī tv evābhaviṣyad iti
uta hainam uvāca naitad api prasnāntam iva hvayantv iti
tad vai nānūktā iti hovāca
atha haike 'bhyudite 'py eva nililyire
te hāparāṃ rātriṃ sametya tuṣṭuvur iyaṃ vāva sā yā naḥ pūrvātyagād iti
te ha rarādhuḥ
te ya evaṃ vidvāṃsaḥ kurvanti rādhnuvanty eva
yadi prātassavanāt somo 'tiricyeta gaur dhayati marutām iti mādhyaṃdinasya pavamānasya purastāt stuyuḥ
gāyatrīṣu stuvanti
gāyatrāddhi savanāt somo 'tiricyate
marutvatīṣu stuvanti
marutvaddhi savanam abhi somo 'tiricyate
dhayadvatīṣu stuvanti
marutām evainad gāvo dhayanti
yāvad ājyānāṃ stotraṃ tāvat stotraṃ bhavati
yata evātiricyate tad evāvakalpayanti
yadi mādhyaṃdināt savanāt somo 'tiricyeta baṇ mahaṃ asi sūryety ārbhavasya pavamānasya purastāt stuyuḥ
bṛhatīṣu stuvanti
bārhatāddhi savanāt somo 'tiricyate
saurīṣu stuvanti
sauryaṃ hi savanam abhi somo 'tiricyate
yāvat pṛṣṭhānāṃ stotraṃ tāvat stotraṃ bhavati
yata evātiricyate tad evāvakalpayanti
yadi tṛtīyasavanāt somo 'tiricyetokthyaṃ kurvīran
yady ukthyam atiricyeta ṣoḍaśinaṃ gṛhṇīran
yadi ṣoḍaśinam atiricyetātirātraṃ kurvīran
rātriṃ ha tvāva nātiricyate svakāmena
paśukāmaḥ paśūn abhyatirecayet
vaiśyasya paśumataḥ paśūn abhyatirecayet
triṣṭupsu stuvanti bṛhatsāma
kṣatraṃ vai triṣṭup
kṣatriya u vai paśūnāṃ pradātā
sa yaḥ paśūnāṃ pradātā sa naḥ paśūn prayacchād iti
atiriktam anubudhyante
atha brūyān mānuvaṣaṭkāra iti
tān sarvahuto hutvābhyutpūryānuvaṣaṭkāre juhuyāt
yady u bhūyān evātiricyeta sahaiva kalaśena pratitiṣṭhet
yadi rājānam avavarṣed indur indum avāgāt tasya ta indav indriyāvato madhumato vicakṣaṇasyopahūtasyopahūto bhakṣayāmi vāg juṣāṇā somasya tṛpyatv iti
tad āhuḥ kṛtsnaṃ vā etad amṛtam annādyam imaṃ lokam āgacchati yad āpaḥ
kṛtsnaṃ vāvedam amṛtam annādyam imaṃ lokam āgād ity eva manyamāno bhakṣayet
saiva tatra prāyaścittiḥ
yadi camasam abhyupākuryus tam uttaravargeṇābhiprāvṛtyāsīta
rājā haitad ṛcā mithunībhavati
tam adhvaryuḥ pratyākīrya yann ādāyeyāt
yady u mārjyaḥ syād ya evainaṃ samprati dhiṣṇyaḥ syāt taṃ prati sadaso viyutya prayacchet
taṃ mārjayitvā yadvidhā itare camasās tadvidhaṃ kuryuḥ
saiva tatra prāyaścittiḥ
yadi prātassavane kalaśo dīryeta viśvet tā viṣṇur ā bharad iti vaiṣṇavīr bṛhatīr mādhyaṃdine kuryuḥ
yadi mādhyaṃdine savane kalaśo dīryeta pavasva vājasātaya iti vaiṣṇavīr anuṣṭubha ārbhave pavamāne kuryuḥ
yadi tṛtīyasavane kalaśo dīryetokthyaṃ kṛtvā yat somam indra viṣṇava ity etāsu brahmasāma kuryuḥ
chidraṃ vā etad yajñasya yataḥ kalaśo dīryate
tad viṣṇunaiva yajñenopayacchanti
taddhy asya sadevam
vaṣaṭkāraṇidhanaṃ sāma bhavati
ubhau vā etāv agnī yad iyaṃ ca vaṣaṭkāraś ca
sāmnaivāsyāṃ samiddhe hūyate
śrāyantīyaṃ brahmasāma
sam evainat tacchrīṇanti
yajñāyajñīyam anuṣṭupsu prohanti
vāg vai yajñāyajñīyam
vāg anuṣṭup
vācaivainat tat samardhayanti
vāravantīyam agniṣṭomasāma
indriyaṃ vai vīryaṃ vāravantīyam
indriyeṇaivainat tad vīryeṇa samardhayanti
dīrṇasya parilipsetāpi
atha upasthitam icchet
sa brūyād anyaṃ kalaśam āharateti
tad udīcīnadaśaṃ pavitraṃ vitatya śalkam asyātha rājānam ānayet
athāgrayaṇasya grahasyāścotayet
athaikadhanam avanayet
ekaṃ vā dvau vā yāvad alaṃ manyeta
saiva tatra prāyaścittiḥ
yadi dhruvaḥ pravarteta saṃlikhya nyubjya yacchuddhaṃ tenābhyutpūrayet
yady āgrayaṇo grahaḥ pravartetetarebhyo 'bhyutpūrayet
ātmā vā āgrayaṇo grahaḥ
prāṇā itare
prāṇebhyo vā ātmā sambhavaty ātmano vā prāṇāḥ
sa eṣa sarvāṇi savanāni pariśaye yajñasyaivāriṣṭyai
yadi pṛṣadājyaṃ pravartetābhyutpūrya punar gṛhṇīyāt
yadi śvāvalihyād ahaviṣyaṃ vā syāt tad uttaravedyāṃ ninīya mārjayitvā srucam anyad gṛhṇīyāt
yadi nārāśaṃsaṃ sannaṃ camasam abhyunnayeran nāha so huto bhakṣāya no bhakṣito homāya
tam antarā paridhīṃś ca bhasma ca ninayet
hutasya cāhutasya cāhutasya hutasya ca pītāpītasya somasyendrāgnī pibataṃ sutaṃ svāheti yajuṣā haike ninayanti
tūṣṇīm eveti ha smāha śāṭyāyaniḥ
mārjayitvā camasaṃ yenādhvaryur graheṇa pratiṣṭheta tasya lipseta
prāṇaṃ vā etasyopadāsayanti yasya camasam upadāsayanti
prāṇo vai grahaḥ
prāṇenaivainaṃ tat samardhayanti
yadi paryunnayeran punaḥ samavanayadhvam iti brūyād atha tam evānūnnayeran
yady udgāyeyur api teṣām eva sampracchindyuḥ
yadi paribhakṣayeyur upahavam iccheta
yadi bahirvedi carantam abhy astam iyād api vā śrāvayeyur gṛhapatāv upahavam iccheta
prajāpatir vai gṛhapatiḥ
prajāpatinaivainaṃ tad upahvayate
yadi grāvā viśīryeta dyutānasya mārutasya brahmasāmnā stuvīran
yadi vā anyo grāvā syāt tenābhiṣuṇuyuḥ
yadi taṃ na vindeyur audumbaraṃ vā pālāśaṃ vā kṛtvā tenābhiṣuṇuyuḥ
saiva tatra prāyaścittiḥ
yady akrītaṃ rājānam apahareyur ā vettor iccheyuḥ
api giriṃ dhāveyuḥ
dīkṣita eva tāvad āsīta
yadi krītam apahareyur yam eva kaṃ cādhigatyābhiṣuṇuyuḥ
yenaivāsya pūrvakrayeṇa krīto bhavati tenaivāsyāyaṃ krīto bhavati
somavikrayiṇe tu kiṃcit kaṃ deyaṃ nen no 'bhiṣavo hato 'sad iti
yadi taṃ na vindeyur babhrutūlāni phālgunāny abhiṣuṇuyuḥ
indro vṛtraṃ vajreṇāhan
tasya yo nastaḥ somo niradravat tāny eva babhrutūlāni phālgunāny abhavan
atha yo vapāyā utkhedanatas tāni rohitatūlāni
tasmād babhrutūlāny evābhiṣutyāni medhyatarāṇi
asuryas tenānabhiṣutya ity āhuḥ
asureṣu vā idam agra āsīt
tad devā abhijityātmann akurvata
tasmād abhiṣutya eveti
yadi taṃ na vindeyur ūtīkān abhiṣuṇuyuḥ
indro vṛtraṃ vajreṇādhyasya nāstṛṣīti manyamānaḥ sa ūtīkān eva prāviśat
tasmai ta evotim avindan
ūtir vā etasya naśyati yasya rājānam apaharanti
ūtim evāsmai vindanti
yajñasya vai yatra śiro 'cchidyata tasya yo rasaḥ prāṇedat ta evotīkā abhavan
tam u tad yajñam eva pratyakṣam abhiṣuṇvanti yad ūtīkān
yadi taṃ na vindeyuḥ
śuklāś śādo 'bhiṣuṇuyuḥ
somo vai rājā yad imaṃ lokam ājagāma sa śātsv eva tad uvāsa
sa evāsya sa nyaṅgaḥ
tam eva tad abhiṣuṇvanti
yadi taṃ na vindeyuḥ parṇam abhiṣuṇuyuḥ
somaṃ vai rājānaṃ yat suparṇa ājahāra tasya yat parṇam apatat sa eva parṇo 'bhavat
sa evāsya sa nyaṅgaḥ
tam eva tad abhiṣuṇvanti
yadi taṃ na vindeyur yā eva kāś cauṣadhīr abhiṣuṇuyuḥ
somaṃ vai rājānaṃ yat suparṇa āharan samabhinat tasya yā vipruṣo 'pataṃs tā evemā oṣadhayo 'bhavan
sarvā u ha vai saumyā oṣadhayaḥ
sa evāsya sa nyaṅgaḥ
tam eva tad abhiṣuṇvanti
pratidhuk prātassavane 'vanayec chṛtaṃ mādhyaṃdine savane dadhi tṛtīyasavane
tam u taṃ somam eva pratyakṣaṃ bhakṣayanti yat payaḥ
oṣadhīnāṃ hi sa rasaḥ
pañca dakṣiṇā dadyāt
pāṅkto yajñaḥ
yāvatī yajñasya mātrā tasyām evaitat pratitiṣṭhanti
avabhṛthād udetya punar dīkṣeta
sa yāvad dāsyan syāt tad dadyāt
saiva tatra prāyaścittiḥ
yad arvāk stutam astutaṃ tat
yad atiṣṭutaṃ duṣṣṭutaṃ tat
yat samprati tat stutam
yad arvāk stuyur uttare stotre tāvatīr vopaprastuyur bhūyo'kṣarāsu vā stuvīran
nyūna eva tad atiriktaṃ dadhati mithunatvāya prajananāya
yady atiṣṭuyur uttare stotre tāvatībhir vā na stuvīran kanīyo'kṣarāsu vā stuvīran
atirikta eva vā tan nyūnaṃ dadhati nyūne vātiriktaṃ mithunatvāya prajananāya
pra mithunena jāyate ya evaṃ veda
yad arvāk stuyus trīḍam agniṣṭomasāma kuryuḥ
dve yajñasya chidram apidhattaḥ
sva āyatana ekā bhavati
yady atiṣṭuyuḥ svāram agniṣṭomasāma kuryuḥ
nyūno vai svaraḥ
aty etad recayanti yad atiṣṭuvanti
yad ekayātiṣṭutaṃ virāṭ sā lomaśā
yad dvābhyāṃ stanau tau
yat tisṛbhir dohaḥ saḥ
dogdhā hy eva yat tṛtīyaḥ
yac catasṛbhiḥ stanās te
yat pañcabhir dohaḥ saḥ
dogdhā hy eva pañcamaḥ
ṣaṣṭhyā vā tvai saptamyā vātiṣṭutam
atha prajāpatiḥ prājijaniṣata
sa tapo 'tapyata
sa aikṣata hanta nu pratiṣṭhāṃ janayai
tato yāḥ prajāḥ srakṣye tā etad eva pratiṣṭhāsyanti nāpratiṣṭhitāś carantīḥ pradaghiṣyanta iti
sa imaṃ lokam ajanayad antarikṣalokam amuṃ lokam iti
tān imāṃs trīn lokāñ janayitvābhyaśrāmyat
tān samatapat
tebhyaḥ saṃtaptebhyas trīṇi śukrāṇy udāyann agniḥ pṛthivyā vāyur antarikṣād ādityo divaḥ
sa etāni śukrāṇi punar abhy evātapat
tebhyaḥ saṃtaptebhyas trīṇy eva śukrāṇy udāyann ṛgveda evāgner yajurvedo vāyoḥ sāmaveda ādityāt
sa etāni śukrāṇi punar abhy evātapat
tebhyaḥ saṃtaptebhyas trīṇy eva śukrāṇy udāyan bhūr ity evargvedād bhuva iti yajurvedāt svar iti sāmavedāt
taddha vai trayyai vidyāyai śukram
etāvad idaṃ sarvam
sa yo vai trayīṃ vidyāṃ viduṣo lokaḥ so 'sya loko bhavati ya evaṃ veda
sa vai khalu prajāpatir yajñaṃ sṛṣṭvordhva udakrāmat
sa devān abravīd etena yūyaṃ trayeṇa vedena yajñaṃ tanudhvam iti
te devā anena trayeṇa vedena yajamānā apa pāpmānam aghnata pra svargaṃ lokam ajānan
te 'bruvan yan nu vayam anena trayeṇa vedena yajamānā apa pāpmānam avadhiṣmahi pra svargaṃ lokam ajñāsiṣma
yan nu no 'dyāyaṃ yajño bhreṣaṃ nīyāt kenainaṃ bhiṣajyāmeti
tān prajāpatir abravīd yad vā etasya trayasya vedasya teja indriyaṃ vīryaṃ rasa āsīd idaṃ vā ahaṃ tat samudayaccham iti
etā vyāhṛtīḥ prayacchann etābhir enaṃ bhiṣajyātheti
sa yadi yajña ṛkto bhreṣaṃ nīyād bhūḥ svāheti gārhapatye juhavātha
saiva tatra prāyaścittiḥ
atha yadi yajuṣṭo bhuvaḥ svāhety āgnīdhre juhavātha
saiva tatra prāyaścittiḥ
atha yadi sāmataḥ svaḥ svāhety āhavanīye juhavātha
saiva tatra prāyaścittiḥ
atha yadīṣṭipaśubandheṣu vā darśapūrṇamāsayor vā bhuvaḥ svāhety anvāhāryapacane juhavātha
saiva tatra prāyaścittiḥ
atha yady anupasmṛtāt kuta idam ajanīti bhūr bhuvaḥ svaḥ svāhety āhavanīye juhavātha
saiva tasya sarvasya prāyaścittiḥ
tad yathā śīrṇaṃ tat parvaṇā parva saṃdhāya bhiṣajyed evam evaivaṃ vidvāṃs tat sarvaṃ bhiṣajyati
atha yasyaitad avidvān prāyaścittiṃ karoti yathā śīrṇena śīrṇaṃ saṃdadhyācchīrṇe vā garam adhyādadhyāt tādṛk tat
tasmād u haivaṃvidam eva prāyaścittiṃ kārayeta
tad āhur yad ṛcā hotṛtvaṃ kriyate yajuṣādhvaryavaṃ sāmnodgītho 'tha kena brahmatvaṃ kriyata iti
anayā trayyā vidyayeti ha brūyāt
tasmād u yam eva brahmiṣṭhaṃ manyeta taṃ brahmāṇaṃ kurvīta
sa ha vāva brahmā ya evaṃ veda
tad āhur yat pūrvapakṣaṃ manuṣyāḥ sunvanty aparapakṣaṃ devā atha sattriṇa ubhau pūrvapakṣāparapakṣau sunvanta āsate yo nvāvaikena manuṣyeṇa saṃsunoti taṃ nv eva paricakṣate
atha kiṃ ya ubhayair devamanuṣyaiḥ
kathaṃ teṣāṃ tad asaṃsutaṃ bhavatīti
sa brūyād amuṃ vai lokaṃ manuṣyāḥ pūrvapakṣe vardhayanty amum āpyāyayanty amuṃ prajanayanti
pūrvapakṣe yajamāno vidyād amum idaṃ lokaṃ vardhayāmy amum āpyāyayāmy amuṃ prajanayāmi
devānām anuṣeṇo 'smīti
yo vai śreyaso 'nuṣeṇo bhavati na vai sa riṣyati
imam u vai lokaṃ devā aparapakṣe vardhayantīmam āpyāyayantīmaṃ prajanayanti
aparapakṣe yajamāno vidyād imam idaṃ lokaṃ vardhayāmīmam āpyāyayāmīmaṃ prajanayāmi
manuṣyāṇām anuṣeṇo 'smīti
yo vai śreyaso 'nuṣeṇo bhavati na vai sa riṣyati
atha ha smāha bhāllabeya imaṃ ha vai lokaṃ devā aparapakṣe vardhayantīmam āpyāyayantīmaṃ prajanayanti
tasmāt pra pūrvāḥ prajāḥ paśava oṣadhayo vanaspatayo daghyante 'thāparāḥ kalyāṇītarāḥ kalyāṇītarāḥ pratidhīyanta iti
etaddha tad vidvān uvāca
tad āhur yad rathāhnyaṃ vā nadīṃ vā giribhidam asaṃsavaṃ manyante 'tha sattriṇaḥ sāmānyāṃ śālāyāṃ bahavaḥ sunvanta āsate yadi vai te manyante nānedaṃ yajāmahā iti saṃ tarhi sunvanti
yady u vai manyante gṛhapatim idaṃ yājayāma ity antaritās tarhi yajñād bhavanti
kathaṃ teṣāṃ tan nāneṣṭaṃ bhavati katham asaṃsutam iti
sa brūyāt
prāṇo vai somo rājā
tad yaddhavirdhāne grāvabhiḥ somaṃ rājānam abhiṣutya nānāgrahān gṛhṇanti nānāpravarān pravṛṇate nānā yajanti tenaivaiṣāṃ tan nāneṣṭaṃ bhavati
atho yad evaiṣā samānā satī devatā nānā prajāsu pratiṣṭhitā teno asaṃsutam iti
yo ha tvai saṃsave saṃsavaṃ veda sa haiva saṃsunvator abhibhavati
ayam eva yo 'yaṃ pavata eṣa eva saṃsave saṃsave
etaṃ hi sarve devā anuyanti
tasmād yām eṣa diśaṃ vāti tāṃ diśam oṣadhayo vanaspatayo 'nupratighnate
sa eṣa vā āpaḥ
yadā hy evarcchaty atha varṣaṃs tiṣṭhati
sa eva tāv antareṇāvakāśaḥ
saiva sā nadī giribhid bhavaty asaṃsavāya
tasmād u haivaṃ vidvān apy utkāśe dīkṣeta
sa haiva saṃsunvator abhibhavati
sa etāṃ devatām upatiṣṭheta śivo 'si pra tvā padye namas te 'stu mā mā hiṃsīr yo māṃ dveṣṭi sa ārtim ārcchatv iti
yo haivaivaṃvidaṃ dveṣṭi sa ārtim ārcchati
tad āhuḥ katidhāvakīryamāṇaḥ praviśatīti
caturdheti brūyāt
caturdhā ha vā eṣa praviśati yo 'vakīryata indraṃ balena marutaḥ prāṇena bṛhaspatiṃ brahmavarcasenāgnim evetareṇa sarveṇa
athāśukraḥ pariśiṣyate
tasyaiṣā prāyaścittiḥ
amāvāsyāṃ rātrim agnim upasamādhāya paristīrya pariṣicyaite āhutī juhuyāt
kāmāvakīrṇo 'smy avakīrṇo 'smi kāma kāmāya svāhā
kāmābhidrugdho 'smy abhidrugdho 'smi kāma kāmāya svāheti
so 'ñjaliṃ kṛtvā trir upatiṣṭhatu
saṃ mā siñcantu marutaḥ sam indraḥ saṃ bṛhaspatis saṃ māyam agniḥ siñcatv āyuṣā ca balena ca dīrgham āyuḥ kṛṇotu ma iti
sa yad āha saṃ mā siñcantu maruta iti maruta evāsmai tat punaḥ prāṇaṃ dadati ya evaṃ veda tasmai
sa yad āha sam indra itīndra evāsmai tat punar balaṃ dadāti ya evaṃ veda tasmai
sa yad āha saṃ bṛhaspatir iti bṛhaspatir evāsmai tad brahmavarcasaṃ dadāti ya evaṃ veda tasmai
sa yad āha sam agnir ity agnir evainaṃ tat sarveṇetareṇa samardhayati yenāvakīryamāṇo vyṛdhyate
sa trir abhimantrayate
traya ime lokāḥ
āpnotīmāṃs trīn lokān sarvam āyur ety ava pāpmānaṃ hate gacchati svargaṃ lokam
atha ha vai naimiśīyā iti sattriṇo 'yasthūṇagṛhapatayaḥ sattraṃ niṣeduḥ
teṣāṃ mahendro vyardhayiṣyan markaṭarūpeṇa puroḍāśaṃ pramamātha
atha haiṣāṃ śitibāhur aiṣakṛto 'dhvaryur anūcāna āsa
sa haitaṃ trayyai vidyāyai śukraṃ rasaṃ pravṛḍhaṃ vidāṃcakāra sarvasya prāyaścittiṃ bhūr bhuvaḥ svar ity etābhir vyāhṛtibhiḥ
etā vai vyāhṛtayaḥ sarvaprāyaścittayaḥ
tad yathā vā adaḥ samudro 'nanto 'pāro 'kṣito dyāvāpṛthivī sarva ime lokā evaṃ vā etā vyāhṛtayo 'kṣitāḥ
adugdhā anantā apārā iti
tad yad vai bhūr iti tad ayaṃ lokaḥ
yad bhuva iti tad idam antarikṣam
yat svar iti tad asau lokaḥ
etā vai vyāhṛtaya etā devatāḥ
etā devatā etā vyāhṛtaya ity etaddha tadviduṣaś śitibāhor aiṣakṛtasya naimiśer markaṭaḥ puroḍāśaṃ pramamātha
sa hovāca caturgṛhītam ājyaṃ gṛhītvā vā hara juhomi veti
sa hovāca tad u ha tvam itthaṃ cāmuthā cāsa yadi tvam anūciṣe markaṭaḥ puroḍāśaṃ pramathiṣyati tasya prāyaścittim iti
sa hovāca tad ahāhaṃ vasīyān bhūyāsaṃ yad aham anvabruvy asamājñātasya prāyaścittim ā vā hara juhomi veti
āharāṇīti hovāca mā hauṣīr iti
tam u hājahāra
tad yasyaivaṃ vidvān brahmā bhavati dakṣiṇato hāsyodaṅ yajñaḥ pravaṇo bhavati
dakṣiṇato hāsyodaṅ yajñaḥ pravaṇaḥ saṃtiṣṭhate yasyaivaṃ vidvān brahmā bhavati ya u cainam evaṃ veda ya u cainam evaṃ veda
vāg eṣā yat pṛṣṭhāni
tām etāṃ viprayuñjate
tāṃ viharanti
sā prathamam ahaḥ prāpya rathantaraṃ bhavati
iyam eva pṛthivī
vāg vai rathantaram
saiṣāvadati
sā dvitīyam ahaḥ prāpya bṛhatī bhavati yām imāṃ śreṣṭhī vācaṃ vadatīty avocad iti
sā hi dūrācchrūyate
sā tṛtīyam ahaḥ prāpya vairūpā bhavati yad idaṃ tiryag vāca ehi prehy āharopāharāśaya pāyayeti
sā caturtham ahaḥ prāpya virāḍ bhavati
tūṣṇīṃ niṣadyam
etaddha vai vairājyaṃ vāco yat tūṣṇīṃ niṣadyaṃ yām imāṃ śreṣṭhinas tūṣṇīm āsīnasyaiva jijñāsante
sā pañcamam ahaḥ prāpya śakvarī bhavati yayā praśiṣṭaḥ śaknoti
sā ṣaṣṭham ahaḥ prāpya revatī bhavati yayānnādyaṃ pradīyate
sā na māsi māsy āttavyā
lelibhasyaitad ājānaṃ yām imāṃ lelibhā vācaṃ vadanti
imāṃ vā ayaṃ hyo 'vadad imāṃ pūrvedyur imāṃ pūrvasamām
samānīṃ bata vācaṃ vadati na batainaṃ paryetīti
evaṃ tad yan māsi māsi pṛṣṭhāny upayanti
tad āhuḥ kāṃ devatāṃ dīkṣamāṇā anuniṣīdanti kām anūttiṣṭhantīti
sa brūyād agniṃ devatānāṃ dīkṣamāṇā anuniṣīdanty ādityam anūttiṣṭhantīti
tasmād dīkṣitān sata āhur āsata iti yady api te śayīrann athottiṣṭheyuḥ
agnir hi devānām āsīnānāṃ śreṣṭhaḥ
agnidevatyā hi tarhi bhavanti
tasmād utthitān sata āhur udasthur iti yady api ta āsīrann atho śayīran
ādityo hi devānām utthitānāṃ śreṣṭhaḥ
ādityadevatyā hi tarhi bhavanti
tad āhuḥ ke bhūtvottiṣṭhantīti
sa brūyān manuṣyā bhūtā dīkṣante devā bhūtvottiṣṭhantīti
ta etad ṛgretasaṃ yajūretasaṃ brahmaṇi yonau reto dadhato yanti
agnāv eva tad āhutībhir abhijuhvato yanti
tasmād dīkṣopasatsu vīva glāyanti
taruṇam iva tarhi reto bhavati
tasmād u strī durhṛdinī vīva glāyati
taruṇam iva hi tarhi reto bhavati
tān stutiśastrais trir vardhayanto 'bhiśṛṇvanto yanti
tasmād garbhā anaśnataḥ sambhavanti
atha ha vai trayaḥ pūrve 'gnaya āsur bhūpatir bhuvanapatir bhūtānāṃ patiḥ
ayaṃ vai loko bhūpatir antarikṣaṃ bhuvanapatir asāv eva loko bhūtānāṃ patiḥ
atha hāyaṃ bhūtir nāma
teṣāṃ ha vaṣaṭkāraḥ śīrṣāṇi cicheda
ta imās tisraḥ pṛthivīḥ praviviśuḥ
tasmād yad agnihotrasya vājyasya vāvaskandet tad abhimṛśed bhūpataye svāhā bhuvanapataye svāhā bhūtānāṃ pataye svāheti
eteṣu haivāsyāgniṣu hutam askannaṃ bhavati
atha ha vai trayaḥ pūrva ṛṣaya āsuḥ śūrpaṃyavam adhvānā antarvān kṛṣiḥ solvālāḥ
te ha yajñasya kṛntatrāṇi dadṛśuḥ
tasyaitāḥ prāyaścittīr dadṛśuḥ śaṃ ca ma upa ca ma āyuś ca me bhūyaś ca me yajña śivo me saṃtiṣṭhasva yajña sviṣṭo me saṃtiṣṭhasva yajñāriṣṭo me saṃtiṣṭhasveti
tasmād etā darśapūrṇamāsābhyāṃ vā cāturmāsyair vā paśubandhena vā saumyena vādhvareṇeṣṭvopariṣṭāj japet
yad evātra yajñasya vidhuraṃ bhavati tad eva tena śamayati
prāṇa evāviṣuvato vyāno viṣuvān apāno yad ūrdhvaṃ viṣuvataḥ
apāno vā idaṃ sarvam āharati
tasmād vayaṃ parastād viṣuvato 'rvācaḥ ṣaḍahān upaimaḥ
vicakṣaṇavatīṃ vācaṃ vadati
annaṃ vai vicakṣaṇam
annavatīm eva tad vācaṃ vadati
vicakṣaṇavatīṃ vācaṃ vadati
somo vai vicakṣaṇaḥ
annam u somaḥ
annavatīm eva tad vācaṃ vadati
vicakṣaṇavatīṃ vācaṃ vadati
prāṇo vai vicakṣaṇaḥ
tasya vāg eva mithunam
mithunavatīm eva tad vācaṃ vadati
vicakṣaṇavatīṃ vācaṃ vadati
annaṃ vai vicakṣaṇam
annena hīmāḥ prajā vipaśyanti
tata ābhyaḥ prajābhyo 'nnādyaṃ prayacchati
sa yadāsmai vrataṃ prayacchet sarvam eva vratayet sarvasyānnādyasyāvaruddhyai
yady u pariśiṃṣyād vratapradaṃ brūyād aśāna vā piba veti
yadya u vrataprado 'nucchiṣṭāśī vā syāt pari vā śiṃṣyāt tad adbhir abhyukṣya chāyāyāṃ niṣektavai brūyāt
tad oṣadhībhir abhisaṃchādayitavai brūyāt
tad oṣadhīnāṃ mūlāny upasiñcati
varṣukaḥ parjanyo bhavati yatraivaṃ vidvān dīkṣate
dīkṣitā udaśūśuṣann itīhāhuḥ
sa yadā dīkṣaṇīyeṣṭiḥ saṃtiṣṭheta yadainam adhvaryur abhyañjayed yadā saṃpavayed athaitam ādityam upatiṣṭheta tvaṃ devatā dīkṣitāsi
sā dīkṣamāṇasyendriyaṃ jyaiṣṭhyaṃ śraiṣṭhyaṃ yaśa ādatse
mā ma indriyaṃ jyaiṣṭhyaṃ śraiṣṭhyaṃ yaśa ādithāḥ
tava dīkṣām anudīkṣa iti
tasyaiṣā devatā dīkṣamāṇasyendriyaṃ jyaiṣṭhyaṃ śraiṣṭhyaṃ yaśo nādatte
sa trivṛd rathantarasāmā bhavati
brahma vai trivṛd brahma rathantaram
brahmaṇā vāva sa tad brahmavarcasam ārdhnot
brahmaṇaiva brahmavarcasam ṛdhnoti ya evaṃ veda
tasya trayastriṃśad dakṣiṇā bhavanti
trayastriṃśad vai devatāḥ
devatānām eva purodhām āśnuta
aśvaś catustriṃśaḥ
prajāpater vā etad rūpaṃ yad aśvaḥ
saprajāpatikānām eva tena devatānāṃ purodhām āśnuta
tasyaitā yathāpūrvam anusavanaṃ dakṣiṇā dadāty aṣṭau prātassavane dadāty ekādaśa mādhyaṃdine savane dvādaśa tṛtīyasavane 'nūbaṃdhyāyām ekām
udavasānīyāyām ekām
anusavanam aśvaṃ tṛtīyaśaḥ
tad yā aṣṭau prātassavane dadāty aṣṭau vasavo vasūnām eva purodhām āśnuta
atha yā ekādaśa mādhyaṃdine savana ekādaśa rudrā rudrāṇām eva tena purodhām āśnuta
atha yā dvādaśa tṛtīyasavane dvādaśādityā ādityānām eva tena purodhām āśnuta
atha yām anūbaṃdhyāyām ekāṃ mitrāvaruṇayor eva tena purodhām āśnuta
atha yām udavasānīyāyām ekāṃ karma karma me dakṣiṇāvad asad iti
atha yam anusavanam aśvaṃ tṛtīyaśaḥ prajāpater eva tena purodhām āśnuta
triśīrṣā ha vai tvāṣṭra āsa
tasya ha trīṇi mukhāny āsus somapānam ekaṃ surāpānam ekam annādanam ekam
prastauti ha smaikenaikena gāyati pratiharaty ekenāśrāvayaty ekena pratyāśrāvayaty ekena śaṃsaty ekena
sa ha smaikāky evānuparisarpaṃ sarvaṃ yajñaṃ saṃsthāpayati
sa heyadvīryāvān āsa
sa u hāsurīputra āsa
sa ha sma pratyakṣaṃ devebhyo vadati parokṣam asurebhyaḥ
yasmā u ha vā bhūyaḥ kāmayate tasmai parokṣaṃ vadati
tasmād u hendro bibhayāṃcakāra yac cāsurīputra āsa yad u ceyadvīryāvān āsa
sa hekṣāṃcakre 'suryo vā ayam āsurīputraḥ
sa pratyakṣam asmabhyaṃ vadati parokṣam asurebhyaḥ
hantainaṃ hanānīti
tasya ha vajreṇa śīrṣāṇi pracicheda
tāny eva vayāṃsy abhavan
tad yat somapānam āsīt sa kapiñjalo 'bhavat
tasmāt sa babhrur iva
babhrur iva hi somaḥ
atha yat surāpānam āsīt sa kalaviṅko 'bhavat
tasmāt sa matta ivāvakrandati
atha yad annādanam āsīt sa tittirir abhavat
tasmāt sa bahurūpa iva
bahurūpam iva hy annam
tasmād u tasya vṛścikaś śaṅkuliṣṭha ity etad annam
sa tvaṣṭā hataputro 'pendraṃ somam ājahre
sa indra īkṣāṃcakre 'smācced vai mā yajñād antarety antarito vai tathā yajñād bhavāni hantainaṃ hanānīti
taṃ ha vajrahasto 'bhidudrāva
sa tvaṣṭā pratyaṅ patitvā patnīḥ prapede
taṃ ha tatra nānuprapede
tasmāt tvaṣṭāraṃ patnīṣu saṃyajanti
tasmād u patnīḥ prapannaṃ na hanyāt
udeyāyendraḥ
sa havirdhānayor eva droṇakalaśe somaṃ rājānaṃ saṃpavitum upeyāya
taṃ ha droṇakalaśenaiva pratidhāya pītvā pravavrāja
anūdeyāya tvaṣṭā
sa ha papracchāsti kiṃcit pariśiṣṭā3m iti
asty ayaṃ saṃsrāva iti hocuḥ
taṃ hāgnau pravartayāṃcakārendraśatrur vardhasva svāheti
taṃ yat prāvartayat sa eva vṛtro 'bhavat
sa vartamāna evāgnīṣomāv abhisaṃbabhūva
tasmād āhur agnīṣomāv asuryāv iti
sa ha smeṣumātram ūrdhvam udardati
tato ha smānāvacchāṃ kṣitiḥ
sa trayīṃ vidyāṃ sarvāṃ śriyaṃ sarvam annādyam api yad idaṃ trirātre sahasraṃ procyate tad abhisaṃbabhūva
tasya hedaṃ sarvaṃ balikṛd āsa
kīlālaṃ ha smāsmai nadyo vahanti
atha hābhiyugvāno nāmāṣṭau devānāṃ sahacarā āsur aṣṭau pitṝṇām aṣṭau manuṣyāṇām aṣṭāv asurāṇām
teṣāṃ ha smendro māyayāṣṭamo bhavati vṛtraṃ jighāṃsan
tasmād u hainam indra eva jaghāna yad indraśatrur vardhasva svāheti pravartayāṃcakāra atha yaddha prāvartayiṣyad indrasya śatrur vardhasva svāheti
indro vai marutaḥ sahasram ajinot svāṃ viśaṃ somāya rājñe pratiprocya
tadanukṛtīdam apy etarhi rājñe pratiprocya viśaṃ jinvanti
tad yamo 'nvabudhyata sahasram ajyāsiṣṭām iti
sa āgacchat
sa etyābravīd upa māsmin sahasre hvayethām iti
tatheti
tam upāhvayetām
sa yamo 'smin sahasre 'pi gām apaśyat sahasrasya gavāṃ payo bibhratīm
tām abravīd iyam eva mama yuvayor etad itarad iti
tāv itarāv abrūtāṃ yad vāva tvam etasyāṃ paśyasi tad āvaṃ paśyāva iti so 'bravīt tayā vā etā eva vikaravāmahā iti
te tayaiva vyakurvata
te 'bruvann aṃśān āharāmahai yasmai naḥ prathamaiṣyati
te 'ṃśān āharanta
somasya prathamait
athendrasyātha yamasya
tām apsu prāveśayan
tām abruvan somāyodehi tṛtīyena cātmanas tṛtīyena ca sahasrasyeti
sā babhruḥ piṅgākṣy udait tṛtīyena cātmanas tṛtīyena ca sahasrasya
saiṣā somakrayaṇī
tṛtīyena ca ha vai tasyai tṛtīyena ca sahasrasya saha somo rājā krīto bhavati
tām punar evāpsu prāveśayan
tām abruvann indrāyodehi tṛtīyena cātmanas tṛtīyena ca sahasrasyeti
sā śabalī paṣṭhauhy udait tṛtīyena cātmanas tṛtīyena ca sahasrasya
saiṣendreṣyā dīyate
tṛtīyena ca ha vai tasyai tṛtīyena ca sahasrasya saha sā dattā bhavati
tām punar evāpsu prāveśayan
tām abruvan yamāyodehi tṛtīyena cātmanas tṛtīyena ca sahasrasyeti
sā dhūmrā dityauhy udaid īrmato hrasīyasī paścād varṣīyasī jaratīva kuṣṭhāśṛṅgī tṛtīyena cātmanas tṛtīyena ca sahasrasya
saiṣānustaraṇī
tṛtīyena ca ha vai tasyai tṛtīyena ca sahasrasya saha sānustaraṇī kṛtā bhavati
no hācakrur iva manyeta
tad āhur nāmuṣmin loke sahasrasyāvakāśo 'sti
ātmane vaiva na vātmane caneti
tad āhuḥ kiyad ita svargo loka iti
yāvat sahasraṃ gaur gavy adhi pratiṣṭhitā tāvad iti brūyāt
atho yāvat sahasraṃ prāṇaiḥ saṃ prāṇantīty atho yāvat sahasram āśvīnānīty atho yāvat sahasraṃ yojanānīty atho yāvat sahasram ahnyānīti
tad gavā gavaivāpnoti
sā yaiṣā śabalī paṣṭhauhy upainam eṣāmuṣmin loke kāmadughā bhūtvā tiṣṭhate ya evaṃ veda
tārpyaṃ pratyasya dakṣiṇā nayati sahasrasya sayonitāyai
sahasraṃ vai yad asṛjata tasya tārpyam eva yonir āsīt
tad yat tārpyaṃ pratyasya sa dakṣiṇā nayati sayony eva tat sahasraṃ karoti
upa hainaṃ sahasraṃ dadivāṃsaṃ sayonisahasraṃ tiṣṭhate ya evaṃ veda
sā yā sahasratamī syāt tasyai karṇam ājaped iḍe rante mahi viśruti śukre candre havye kāmye 'dite sarasvaty etāni te 'ghnye nāmāni deveṣu naḥ sukṛto brūtād iti
sukṛtaṃ ha vā enaṃ deveṣv āha
tām kalaśam apaghrāpayaty apajighra kalaśaṃ mahyā tvā viśantv indavaḥ sā no dhukṣaḥ sahasram urudhārā payasvatīti
upa hainaṃ sahasraṃ dadivāṃsaṃ sahasraṃ tiṣṭhate ya evaṃ veda
athaite ṣaḍrātrāḥ
maruto vā akāmayantaujiṣṭhā baliṣṭhā bhūyiṣṭhā vīryavattamā devānāṃ syāma jayema svargaṃ lokam iti
ta etaṃ ṣaḍrātraṃ yajñam apaśyan
tam āharan
tenāyajanta
tato vai ta ojiṣṭhā baliṣṭhā bhūyiṣṭhā vīryavattamā devānām āsann ajayan svargaṃ lokam
ojiṣṭho baliṣṭho bhūyiṣṭho vīryavattamaḥ svānāṃ bhavati jayati svargaṃ lokaṃ ya evaṃ veda
pṛṣṭhyena ṣaḍahena yanti
śrīr vai varṣma pṛṣṭhāni
śriyam eva tad varṣma pṛṣṭhāny abhyārohati
ojo vai vīryaṃ pṛṣṭhāni
ojasaiva tad vīryeṇa yanti
svargo vai lokaḥ pṛṣṭhāni
svargam eva tal lokaṃ rohanto yanti
teṣāṃ sarasvatyā upamajjane dīkṣā
dakṣiṇe tīre dīkṣante
cakravatī sadohavirdhāne bhavata ulūkhalabudhno yūpa utkrāntyā anapabhraṃśāya
yaddhi te tatra kurvāṇā ivāsīrann apabhraṃśo haiṣāṃ saḥ
śamyāparāsaṃ yanti
ete ha vai svargasya lokasya vikramā yacchamyāparāsāḥ
svargasyaiva tallokasya vikramān kramamāṇā yanti
ghnanta ākrośanto yanti
etad vai balasya rūpaṃ yaddhatam ākruṣṭam
sarasvatyā yanti
vāg vai sarasvatī
vāg u devayānaḥ panthāḥ
devayānenaiva tat pathā yanti
pratīpaṃ yanti
pratīpam iva vai svargo lokaḥ
svargam eva tallokaṃ pratipadyante
prāñca udañco yanti
prāṅ iva ha vā udaṅ svargo lokaḥ
svargam eva tal lokaṃ rohanto yanti
ā prakṣāt prāsravaṇād yanti
eṣa u ha vai vāco 'nto yat prakṣaḥ prāsravaṇaḥ
yatro ha vai vāco 'ntas tat svargo lokaḥ
svargam evaitallokaṃ gacchanti
ahīnasaṃ hāśvatthiṃ putrā upasametyocuḥ sattrāyāmo vai bhagavo 'nu naḥ śādhīti
sa hovāca maivaṃ vocata
durupadharṣo vai saṃvatsaraḥ
yathā vai rathanābhāv arāḥ pratiṣṭhitā evaṃ vai saṃvatsare sarve mṛtyavaḥ pratiṣṭhitāḥ
athaitad evaṃ brūtheti
te hocus teṣāṃ vai tvam eva bhiṣag asi tvaṃ prāyaścittir anv eva naḥ śādhīti
taddhāsya priyam āsa
sa hovācaivaṃ ced brūtha ṣaṭsu sma pratiṣṭhāsu pratitiṣṭhata
ṣaḍbhya sma haritmatībhyo meta
catuścakraṃ sma pārayiṣṇuṃ samārohata
svargasya sma lokasya patho 'ñjasāyanān meta
saṃvatsarasya sma vyāptam atiplavadhvam
daivyaṃ sma mithunam upeta
praspaṣṭāt sma sārthān mā hīyadhvam
acyutaṃ sma yajñasya mā cyāvayata
yajñasya sma śvastanam upeta
vācaṃ sma satyavatīm upeta
varṣiṣṭhān smājau yuṅgdhvam uttarāvatīṃ sma śriyam upeta
svarge sma loke pratitiṣṭhata
grāmāt smāraṇyaṃ meta
jñānāt smāvirbhavān meta
daivyāt sma vivāhān meta
yajñāt sma meteti
etāni hainān anuśaśāsa
te hocur anu na idam aśiṣaḥ parokṣeṇeva
tathā no 'nuśādhi yathedaṃ vijānīyāmeti
tāsu cyāvanam
cyavano vai bhārgavo vāstupasya brāhmaṇam avet
sa putrān abravīd vāstupasya vai brāhmaṇaṃ veda
taṃ mā vāstau nidhāya triḥ punaḥprayāṇaṃ prayāteti
te 'bruvan na śakṣyāma ākrośanavanto bhaviṣyāmaḥ
pitaram ahāsiṣur iti no vakṣyantīti
neti hovāca tena vai yūyaṃ vasīyāṃso bhaviṣyatha teno eva mama punaryuvatāyā āśā
hitvaiva mā prayāteti tān ajñāpayat
taṃ sarasvatyai śaiśave nidhāya triḥ punaḥprayāṇaṃ prāyan
so 'kāmayata vāstau hīnaḥ punar yuvā syāṃ kumārīṃ jāyāṃ vindeya sahasreṇa yajeyeti
sa etat sāmāpaśyat
tenāstuta
taṃ tuṣṭuvānaṃ śaryāto mānavo grāmeṇādhyavāsyat
taṃ kumārā gopālā avipālā mṛdā śakṛtpiṇḍair āsapāṃsubhir adihan
so 'saṃjñāṃ śāryātyebhyo 'karot
tan na mātā putram ajānān na putro mātaram
so 'bravīccharyāto mānavaḥ kim ihābhitaḥ kiṃcid adrāṣṭa yata idam ittham abhūd iti
tasmai hocur na nu tato 'nyat sthavira evāyaṃ niṣṭhāvaḥ śete
tam adya kumārā gopālā avipālā mṛdā śakṛtpiṇḍair āsapāṃsubhir adhikṣan
tata idam ittham abhūd iti
sa hovāca cyavano vai sa bhārgavo 'bhūt
sa vāstupasya brāhmaṇaṃ veda
taṃ nūnaṃ putrā vāstau hitvā prāyāsiṣur iti
tam ādrutyābravīd ṛṣe namas te 'stu
śāryātyebhyo bhago mṛḍeti
atha ha sukanyā śāryātyā kalyāṇy āsa
sa hovāca sa vai me sukanyāṃ dehīti
neti hovāca
anyad dhanaṃ brūṣveti
neti hovāca
vāstupasya vai brāhmaṇaṃ veda
tāṃ ma ihopanidhāyāsāyam evādya grāmeṇa yātād iti
te vai tvā mantrayitvā pratibravāmeti
te hocur mantrayitvā ekaṃ vai dve trīṇi paramam anayā dhanāni labhemahy athainayeha sarvam eva lapsyāmahe
hantāsmā imāṃ dadāmeti
tāṃ hāsmai daduḥ
tāṃ hocuḥ kumāri sthaviro vā ayaṃ niṣṭhāvo nālam anusaraṇāya
yadaiva vayaṃ yunajāmahā athānvādhāvatād iti
sā heyaṃ yuktaṃ grāmam anusariṣyanty anūttasthau
sa hovācāhe paridhāva sakhāyaṃ jīvahāyinam iti
sā yadītīyāya yadīti
kṛṣṇasarpa u haivaināṃ pratyuttasthau
sā ha tad eva nirvidyopaviveśa
atha hāśvinau darvihomiṇau bhiṣajyantāv idaṃ ceratur anapisomau
tau hainām etyocatuḥ kumāri sthaviro vā ayam asarvo nālaṃ patitvanāyāvayor jāyaidhīti
neti hovāca
yasmā eva mā pitādāt tasya jāyā bhaviṣyāmīti
taddhāyam ājughoṣa
atha hemau preyatuḥ
sa hovāca kumāri ko nv eṣa ghoṣo 'bhūd iti
puruṣau memāv upāgātāṃ yat kalyāṇatamaṃ rūpāṇāṃ tena rūpeṇeti
tau tvā kim avocatām iti
kumāri sthaviro vā ayam asarvo nālaṃ patitvanāyāvayor jāyaidhīti
sā tvaṃ kim avoca iti
nety aham avocaṃ yasmā eva mā pitādāt tasya jāyā bhaviṣyāmīti
taddhāsya priyam āsa
sa hovācāśvinau vai tau darvihomiṇau bhiṣajyantāv idaṃ carato 'napisomau
tau tvaitad evāgatya śvo vaktārau
tau tvaṃ brūtād yuvaṃ vā asarvau stho yau devau santāv asomapau sthaḥ
sarvo vai mama patir yaḥ somapa iti
tau vai tvā vaktārau kas tasyeśe yad āvam apisomau syāveti
ayaṃ mama patir iti brūtāt
teno eva me punaryuvatāyā āśeti
tau haināṃ śvobhūta etyaitad evocatuḥ
sā hovāca yuvaṃ vā asarvau stho yau devau santāv asomapau sthaḥ
sarvo vai mama patir yaḥ somapa iti
tau hocatuḥ kas tasyeśe yad āvam apisomau syāveti
ayaṃ mama patir iti hovāca
vatsaiḥ paśūn saṃvāśayanti
yadā vai paśavo vatsaiḥ saṃvāśante 'tha kāmān duhre
kāmadughā asmai revatayo bhavanti
pavamāne saṃvāśayed yaḥ kāmayetāmuṣmin me loke kāmadughāḥ syur iti
amuṣmin haivāsya loke kāmadughā bhavanti
abhyāvartiṣu saṃvāśayed yaḥ kāmayetāsmin me loke kāmadughāḥ syur iti
asmin haivāsya loke kāmadughā bhavanti
ubhayatra saṃvāśayed yaḥ kāmayetobhayor me lokayoḥ kāmadughāḥ syur iti
ubhayor haivāsya lokayoḥ kāmadughā bhavanti
tad āhur ito vatsā syur ito mātaraḥ
udīcīr vā āpaḥ syandante
āpo vā ete yat paśava iti
tad u vā āhur ita eva vatsāḥ syur ito mātaraḥ
yadā vai pitā putraṃ niravasāyayaty uttarato vāva sa taṃ niravasāyayati
tasmād uttarato vatsāḥ syur dakṣiṇato mātaraḥ
devāsurāḥ paśuṣv aspardhanta
te devā vatsair uttarato 'tiṣṭhann athāsurā mātṛbhir dakṣiṇataḥ
tā mātaro nirdīrya vatsān abhipalāyanta
adhārayan devā vatsān
tāḥ samākramyāsurāṇām avṛñjata
tābhir udañcaḥ prādravan
vṛṅkte dviṣato bhrātṛvyasya paśūn ya evaṃ veda
tasmād uttarata eva vatsāḥ syur dakṣiṇato mātara iti
ṛṣayo vai satrād utthāyāyanta āyuñjānāḥ
te hocur eta kiṃcid eva yakṣaṃ paśyāmeti
te hocur akūpāro vā ayaṃ kaśyapaḥ samudre 'ntar mahad yakṣam
eta taṃ paśyāmeti
taṃ hānvabhyaveyuḥ
tebhyo ha nāvir āsa
te hocur etendram eva stavāma sa vāvāsyeśe
sa eva na imaṃ darśayiṣyatīti
te 'trim abruvann ṛṣe tvaṃ stutād iti
sa etam atris tṛcam apaśyat
tenainam upāyan
yad indra citra ma iha nāsti tvādātam adrivaḥ
rādhas tan no vidadvasa ubhayāhasty ā bhara
iti
sa hekṣāṃcakre mahad bata ma ṛṣayo yācanti
ubhayāhasty ā bhareti vā āhur iti
yat te dikṣu prarādhyaṃ mano asti śrutaṃ bṛhat
tena dṛḍhā cid adriva ā vājaṃ darṣi sātaye
iti
sa hekṣāṃcakre dṛḍhaṃ bata ma ṛṣayo yācanti
na hājajñāv akūpāraṃ didṛkṣanta iti
yan manyase vareṇyam indra dyukṣaṃ tad ā bhara
vidyāma tasya te vayam akūpārasya dāvane
iti
sa hājajñāv akūpāraṃ vai didṛkṣanta iti
taṃ ha padodasyann uvācedam eva medam ṛṣayo mahad ivobhayāhasty ā bharety avocann iti
tam apaśyan
tā etāḥ kāmasanaya ṛcaḥ
etaṃ vai te kāmam akāmayanta
sa ebhyaḥ kāmaḥ samārdhyata
yatkāma evaitābhir ṛgbhi stute sam asmai sa kāma ṛdhyate
athākūpāram
akūpāro vai kaśyapaḥ kalibhiḥ saha samudram abhyavaiṣat
tasmin pratiṣṭhām aicchat
sa etat sāmāpaśyat
tenāstuta
tato vai sa samudre pratiṣṭhām avindatemām eva pṛthivīm
tato ha sma vai tasya kalayaḥ pṛṣṭha āsate
tad etat pratiṣṭhāsāma
pratitiṣṭhati ya evaṃ veda
samudro vai chandomāḥ
kaśyapo vai samudram atipārayitum arhati
tad yad atrākūpāraṃ bhavati samudrasyaivātipāraṇāya
yad v akūpāraḥ kaśyapo 'paśyat tasmād ākūpāram ity ākhyāyate
athaitā dvipado bhavanty uktabrāhmaṇāḥ
tā etā bhavanti pavasva soma mahe dakṣāyeti
mahaddhy etad ahar yad aṣṭācatvāriṃśam
tāsu vidharmoktabrāhmaṇam
tac caturakṣaraṇidhanaṃ bhavati catuṣpadā vai paśavaḥ
paśavaś chandomāḥ paśūnām evāvaruddhyai
upo ṣu jātam apturam iti janadvatīr bhavanti
janadvad vai jagatyai rūpam
jāgatam etad ahaḥ
gobhir bhaṃgaṃ pariṣkṛtam
induṃ devā ayāsiṣuḥ
arṣā nas soma śaṃ gave dhukṣasva pipyuṣīm iṣam
vardhā samudram ukthyam
iti gomatīḥ paśumatīr bhavanti paśūnām evāvaruddhyai
paśavo hi chandomāḥ
tam id vardhantu no gira iti vṛddhaṃ hy etad ahar yad aṣṭācatvāriṃśam
tad yathā vṛkṣaṃ vā giriṃ vādhiruhya vyavekṣetaivam evaitasmāllokād anyān lokān vyavekṣate
sa imāḥ prajā aśanāyantīḥ pratyavaikṣata
tā dvābhyāṃ rūpābhyāṃ pratyādravan nīlena ca suvarṇena ca
tad yat parjanyasya varṣiṣyataḥ kṛṣṇaṃ tannīlam
atha yad apsv antar vidyotate tat suvarṇam
tābhyo 'varṣat
tata odano 'jāyata
tam aśitvodānan
sa udano 'bhavat
tad udanasyodanatvam
udano ha vai nāmaiṣa
tam odana iti parokṣam ācakṣate
dvitīyaṃ jyāyo 'nnādyam ajāyata
tad abhisaṃpadya vyamathnata
sa mantho 'bhavat
tan manthasya manthatvam
tad etad dvayam evānnādyasya rūpaṃ yaccaivāśnāti yacca pibati
yad aśnāty odanasya tad rūpaṃ yat pibati manthasya tat
ubhayaṃ hāsyaitad gṛhe 'dhigamyate ya evaṃ veda
tau haitau prajāpater eva stanau yad vrīhiś ca yavaś ca
tābhyām imāḥ prajā bibharti
